[[subhāṣitāvaliḥ	Source: EB]]
[








vallabhadevakṛta-subhāṣitāvaliḥ


0001-1 tāṃ bhavānīṃ bhavānītakleśanāśaviśāradāṃ |
0001-2 śāradāṃ śāradāṃ bhodasitaṃsihāsanāṃ numaḥ | |
0002-1 anapekṣitaguruvacanā sarvāngranthīnvibhedayati samyak |
0002-2 prakaṭayati pararahasyaṃ vimarśaśaktirnijā jayati | |
0003-1 dikkālādyanavacchinnānantacinmātramūrtaye |
0003-2 svānubhūtyekamānāya namaḥ śāntāya tejase | |
0004-1 jagatsisṛkṣāpralayakriyāvidhau
0004-2 prayatnamunmeṣanimeṣavibhramaṃ |
0004-3 vadanti yasyekṣaṇalolapakṣmaṇāṃ
0004-4 parāya tasmai parameṣṭhine namaḥ | |
0005-1 namastribhuvanotpattisthitisaṃhārahetave |
0005-2 viṣṇavepārasaṃsārapārottaraṇasetave | |
0006-1 surāsuraśiroratnakāntivicchuritāṅghraye |
0006-2 namastribhuvaneśāya haraye siṃharūpiṇe | |
0007-1 namastasmai varāhāya helayoddharate mahīṃ |
0007-2 khuramadhyagato yasya meruḥ khurakhurāyate | |
0008-1 namastuṅgaśiraścumbicandracāmaracārave |
0008-2 trailokyanagarārambhamūlastambhāya śaṃbhave | |
0009-1 abhipretārthasiddhyarthaṃ pūjito yaḥ surairapi |
0009-2 sarvavighnacchide tasmai gaṇādhipataye namaḥ | |
0010-1 nitambālasagāminyaḥ pīnonnatapayodharāḥ |
0010-2 manmathāya namastasmai yasyāyatanamaṅganāḥ | |
0011-1 anantamāmadheyāya sarvākaravidhāyine |
0011-2 samastamantravācyāya viśvaikapataye namaḥ | |
0012-1 oṃ namaḥ paramārthaikarūpāya paramātmane |
0012-2 svecchāvabhāsitāsatyabhedabhinnāya śaṃbhave | |
0013-1 kulaśailadalaṃ pūrṇasuvarṇagirikarṇikaṃ |
0013-2 namodhitiṣṭhatenantanālaṃ kamalaviṣṭaraṃ | |
0014-1 karṇikādiṣviva svarṇamarṇavādiṣvivodakaṃ |
0014-2 bhediṣvabhedi yattasmai parasmai mahase namaḥ | |
0015-1 namo vāṅmanasātītamahimne parameṣṭhine |
0015-2 triguṇāṣṭaguṇānantaguṇannirguṇamūrtaye | |
0016-1 namaḥ śivāya niḥśeṣakleśapraśamaśāline |
0016-2 triguṇagranthidurbhedabhavabandhavibhedine | |
0017-1 samastalakṣaṇāyoga eva yasyopalakṣaṇaṃ |
0017-2 tasmai namostu devāya kasmaicidapi śaṃbhave | |
0018-1 saṃsāraikanimittāya saṃsāraikavirodhine |
0018-2 namaḥ saṃsārarūpāya niḥsaṃsārāya śaṃbhave | |
0019-1 yathā tathāpi yaḥ pūjyo yatra tatrāpi yorcitaḥ |
0019-2 yopi vā sopi vā yosau devastasmai namostu te | |
0020-1 sadasattvena bhāvānāṃ yuktā yā dvitayī sthitiḥ |
0020-2 tāmullaṅghya tṛtīyasmai namaścitrāya śaṃbhave | |
0021-1 namaḥ svatantracicchaktimudritasvavibhūtaye |
0021-2 avyaktavyaktarūpāya kasmaicinmantramūrtaye | |
0022-1 āsannāya sudūrāya guptāya prakaṭātmane |
0022-2 sulabhāyātidurgāya namaścitrāya śaṃbhave | |
0023-1 carācarajagatsphārasphurattāmātradharmiṇe |
0023-2 durvijñeyarahasyāya yuktairapyātmane namaḥ | |
0024-1 viṣṇurvā tripurāntako bhavatu vā brahmā surendrothavā
0024-2 bhānurvā śaśalakṣaṇotha bhagavānbuddhotha siddhothavā |
0024-3 rāgadveṣaviṣārtimoharahitaḥ sattvānukampodyato
0024-4 yaḥ sarvaiḥ saha saṃskṛto guṇaguṇaistasmai namaḥ sarvadā | |
0025-1 ślokoyaṃ svāmidattasya tatsmṛtyai kāvyalakṣitaḥ |
0025-2 yokarotkavināmāṅkaṃ cakrapāṇiyayābhidhaṃ | |
0026-1 bhavabījāṅkurajaladā rāgādyāḥ kṣayamupāgatā yasya |
0026-2 brahmā vā viṣṇurvā haro jino vā namastasmai | |
0027-1 kastūrītilakaṃ lalāṭaphalake vakṣaḥsthale kaustubhaṃ
0027-2 nāsāgre navamauktikaṃ karatale veṇuṃ kare kaṅkaṇaṃ |
0027-3 sarvāṅge haricandanaṃ suvimalaṃ kaṇṭhe ca muktāvalīṃ
0027-4 bibhratstrīpariveṣṭito vijayate gopālacūḍāmaṇiḥ | |
0028-1 aviratāmbujasaṃgatisaṃgaladbahalakesarasaṃvaliteva vaḥ |
0028-2 lalitavastuvidhānasukhollasattanuruhā tanurātmabhuvovatāt | |
0029-1 lakṣmīkapolasaṃkrāntakāntapattralatojjvalāḥ |
0029-2 dordrumāḥ pāntu vaḥ śaurerghanacchāyā mahāphalāḥ | |
0030-1 pātu vo medinīdolā balendudyutitaskarī |
0030-2 daṃṣṭrā mahāvarāhasya pātalagṛhadīpakā | |
0031-1 madamayamadamayaduragaṃ yamunāmavatīrya vīryaśālī yaḥ |
0031-2 mama ratimamaratiraskṛtiśamanapuraḥ sa kriyātkṛṣṇaḥ | |
0032-1 sa pātu vo yasya hatāvaśeṣās
0032-2 tattulyavarṇāñjanarañjiteṣu |
0032-3 vālaṇyayukteṣvapi vitrasanti
0032-4 daityāḥ svakāntānayanotpaleṣu | |
0033-1 caṇḍacāṇūradordaṇḍamaṇḍalīkhaṇḍamaṇḍitaṃ |
0033-2 avyādvo bālaveṣasya viṣṇorgopatanorvapuḥ | |
0034-1 govardhanoddharaṇahṛṣṭasamastagopa-
0034-2 nānāstutiśravaṇalajjitamānasasya |
0034-3 smṛtvā varāhavapurindukalāprakāśa-
0034-4 daṃṣṭroddhṛtakṣiti hareravatu smitaṃ vaḥ | |
0035-1 manthakṣmādharaghūrṇitārṇavapayaḥ pūrāntarālollasal-
0035-2 lakṣmīkandalak_oṃalāṅgadalanaprādurbhavatsaṃbhramāḥ |
0035-3 harṣotkaṇṭakitatvaco madhuripordevāsurākarṣaṇa-
0035-4 vyāpāroparamāya pāntu jagatīmābaddhavīpsā giraḥ | |
0036-1 pṛṣṭhabhrāmyadamandamandaragirigrāvāgrakaṇḍūyanān-
0036-2 nidrāloḥ kamaṭhākṛterbhagavataḥ śvāsānilāḥ pāntu vaḥ |
0036-3 yatsaṃskārakalānuvartanavaśādvelānibhenāmbhaso
0036-4 yātāyātamatandritaṃ jalanidhernādyāpi viśrāmyati | |
0037-1 kiṃcitkuñcitalocanasya pibataḥ paryāptamekaṃ stenaṃ
0037-2 sadyaḥprasrutadughavindumaparaṃ hastena saṃmārjataḥ |
0037-3 mātraikāṅgulilālitasya cibuke smerānanasyānanā-
0037-4 cchaureḥ kṣīrakaṇāvalīva patitā dantadyutiḥ pātu vaḥ | |
0038-1 kālindīpulinodareṣu musalī yāvadgataḥ krīḍituṃ
0038-2 tāvatkarburikāpayaḥ piba hare vardhiṣyate te śikhā |
0038-3 itthaṃ bālatayā pratāraṇaparāḥ śrutvā yaśodāgiraḥ
0038-4 pāyādvaḥ svaśikhāṃ spṛśanpramuditaḥ kṣīrerdhapīte hariḥ | |
0039-1 ānandena yaśodayā samadanaṃ gopāṅganābhiściraṃ
0039-2 sāśaṅkaṃ balavidviṣā sakusumaṃ siddhaiḥ pṛthivyākulaṃ |
0039-3 serṣyaṃ gopakumārakaiḥ sakaruṇaṃ pauraiḥ suraiḥ sasmitaṃ
0039-4 yo dṛṣṭaḥ sa punātu vo madhuripuḥ protkṣipragovardhanaḥ | |
0040-1 kṛṣṇenāmba gatena rantumadhunā mṛdbhakṣitā svecchayā
0040-2 satyaṃ kṛṣṇa ka evamāha musalī mithyāmba paśyānanaṃ |
0040-3 vyādehīti vikāsitetha vadane mātā samastaṃ jagad-
0040-4 dṛṣṭvā yasya jagāma vismayavaśaṃ pāyātsa vaḥ keśavaḥ | |
0041-1 kiṃ yuktaṃ bata māmananyamanasaṃ vakṣaḥsthalasthāyinīṃ
0041-2 bhaktāmapyavadhūya kartuṃ adhunā kāntāsahasraṃ tava |
0041-3 ityuktvā phaṇabhṛtphaṇāmaṇigatāṃ svāmeva matvā tanuṃ
0041-4 nidrāchedakaraṃ hareravatu vo lakṣmyā vilakṣasmitaṃ | |
0042-1 svaprāsāditadarśanāmanunayanprāneśvarīmādarā-
0042-2 daṃsesminpatitairapāṅgavalitairyadbodhitopyaśrubhiḥ |
0042-3 pratyāyyastvamato mayā nanu hare koyaṃ kramavyatyayaḥ
0042-4 pātu tvāṃ vrajayoṣitetyabhihitaṃ lajjākarśārṅgiṇaḥ | |
0043-1 bhaktiprahvavilokanapraṇayiṇī nīlotpalaspardhinī
0043-2 dhyānālambanatāṃ samādhiniratairnīte hitaprāptaye |
0043-3 lāvaṇyasya mahānidhī rasikatāṃ lakṣmīdṛśostanvatī
0043-4 yuṣmākaṃ kurutāṃ bhavārtiharaṇaṃ netre tanurvā hareḥ | |
0044-1 yena dhvastamanobhavena balijitkāyaḥ purāstrīkṛto
0044-2 yaścodvṛttabhujaṃgarahāravalayo gaṅgāṃ ca yodhārayat |
0044-3 yasyāhuḥ śaśimacchiro hara iti stutyaṃ ca nāmāmarāḥ
0044-4 pāpātsa svayamandhakakṣayakarastvāṃ sarvad_oṃādhavaḥ | |
0045-1 kiṃcinnirmucyamāne gagana iva mukhe nāṭyanidrāpayodair-
0045-2 nyakkurvāṇe svabhāsā phaṇipatiśirasāṃ ratnadīpāṃśujālaṃ |
0045-3 pāyāstāṃ vo muroreḥ śaśitapanamaye locane yadvibhāsā
0045-4 lakṣmyā kastasthamardhaṃ vikasati kamalasyārdhamabhyeti nidrāṃ | |
0046-1 mallaiḥ śailendrakalpaḥ śiśurakhilajanaiḥ puṣpacāpoṅganābhir-
0046-2 gopaistu prākṛtātmā divi kuliśabhṛtā viśvakāyoprameyaḥ |
0046-3 kruddhaḥ kaṃsena kālo bhayacakitadṛśā yogibhirdhyeyamūrtir-
0046-4 dṛṣṭo raṅgāvatāre hariramarajanānandakṛtpātu yuṣmān | |
0047-1 bhindannarātihṛdayāni hareḥ punātu
0047-2 niḥśvāsavātamukharīkṛtakoṭaro vaḥ |
0047-3 saṃkrāntakukṣikuharāspadasaptasindhu-
0047-4 saṃghaṭṭaghorataraghoṣa ivāśu śaṅkhaḥ | |
0048-1 pāyātsa vaḥ kumudakundamṛṇālagauraḥ
0048-2 śaṅkho hareḥ karatalāmbarapūrṇacandraḥ |
0048-3 nādena yasya suraśatruvilāsinīnāṃ
0048-4 kāñcyo bhavanti śithilā jaghanasthalīṣu | |
0049-1 dṛṣṭasya yasya hariṇā raṇamūrdhni mūrtir-
0049-2 udbhūtaduḥsahamahaḥprasarā samantāt |
0049-3 tallocanasthitaravipratibimbagarbhe-
0049-4 vābhāti cakramaricakranudestu tadvaḥ | |
0050-1 udvṛttadaityapṛtanāpatikaṇṭhapīṭha-
0050-2 cchedocchaladbahalaśoṇitaśoṇadhāraṃ |
0050-3 cakraṃ kriyādabhimatāni harerudāra-
0050-4 digdāhadāruṇanabhaḥśriyamudvahadvaḥ | |
0051-1 yasyodyadbāṇavāhudrumagahanavanacchedagoṣṭhīkuṭhāraṃ
0051-2 cakraṃ niṣkrāntatīvrānalabahalakaṇākīrṇadhāraṃ vicintya |
0051-3 jātagrāsāvasāyo divasakṛtisalanmāṃsalāṃśupravāhe
0051-4 muhyatyadyāpi rāhuḥ sa dahatu duritānyāśu daityāntako vaḥ | |
0052-1 daityāsthipañjaravidāraṇalabdharandhra-
0052-2 raktāmbunirjarasariddhanajātapaṅkāḥ |
0052-3 bālendukoṭikuṭilāḥ śukacañcubhāso
0052-4 rakṣantu siṃhavapuṣo nakharā harervaḥ | |
0053-1 ādityāḥ kiṃ daśaite pralayabhayakṛtaḥ svīkṛtākāśadeśāḥ
0053-2 kiṃ volkāmaṇḍalāni tribhuvanadahanāyodyatānīti bhītaiḥ |
0053-3 pāyāsurnārasiṃhaṃ vapuramaragaṇairbibhrataḥ śārṅgapāṇer-
0053-4 dṛṣṭvā dṛptāsurorastaladaraṇagaladraktaraktā nakhā vaḥ | |
0054-1 merūrukesaramudāradigantapattram-
0054-2 āmūlalambicalaśeṣaśarīranālaṃ |
0054-3 yenoddhṛtaṃ kuvalayaṃ salilātsalīlam-
0054-4 uttaṃsakārthamiva pātu sa vo varāhaḥ | |
0055-1 na mṛdnīyānmṛdvī kathamiva mahī potranikaṣair-
0055-2 mukhāgnijvālābhiḥ kanakagirirīyānna vilayaṃ |
0055-3 na śuṣyeyuḥ śvāsaiḥ salilanidhayaḥ sapta ca kathaṃ
0055-4 varāho vaḥ pāyāditi vipulacintāparikaraḥ | |
0056-1 svāmī sanbhuvanatrayasya vikṛtiṃ nītosi kiṃ yācñayā
0056-2 yadvā viśvasṛjā tvayaiva na kṛtaṃ taddīyatāṃ te kutaḥ |
0056-3 dānaṃ śreṣṭhatamāya tubhyamatulaṃ bandhāya no muktaye
0056-4 vijñapto balinā niruttaratayā hrīto hariḥ pātu vaḥ | |
0057-1 līne śrotraikadeśe nabhasi nayanayostejasi kvāpi yāte
0057-2 śvāsagrāsopayukte maruti jalanidhau pāyurandhrārdhapīte |
0057-3 potraprāntaikar_oṃāntaravivaragatāṃ mṛgyataḥ śārṅgapāṇeḥ
0057-4 kroḍākārasya pṛthvīmakalitaviṣayaṃ vaibhavaṃ vaḥ punātu | |
0058-1 kvedānīṃ darpitāste ghanamadamadirāmodino digdhipendrā
0058-2 he mero mandarāndre malaya himagire sādhu vaḥ kṣmādharatvaṃ |
0058-3 śeṣa ślāghyosi dīrghaiḥ pṛthubhuvanabharoccaṇḍaśauṇḍaiḥ śirobhiḥ
0058-4 śaṃsansotprāsamuccairiti dharaṇibhṛtaḥ pātu yuṣmānvarāhaḥ | |
0059-1 āvyādvo vāmano yasya kaustubhapratibimbitā |
0059-2 kautukālokinī jātā jāṭharīva jagattrayī | |
0060-1 ekasthaṃ jīviteśe tvayi sakalajagatsāramālokayāmaḥ
0060-2 śyāme cakṣustavāsminvapuṣi niviśate nālpapuṇyasya puṃsaḥ |
0060-3 kasyānyatrāmṛtesminratirativipulā dṛṣṭirevāmṛtaṃ te
0060-4 daityairityucyamāno munibhirapi hariḥ straiṇarūpovatādvaḥ | |
0061-1 bhrāmyanmahāgirinigharṣaṇalabdhapṛṣṭha-
0061-2 kaṇḍūyanakṣaṇasukhāyitagāḍhanidraḥ |
0061-3 suṣvāpa dīrghataraghargharaghoraghoṣaḥ
0061-4 śvāsābhibhūtajaladhiḥ kamaṭhaḥ sa vovyātu | |
0062-1 sa dhūrjaṭijaṭājūṭo jāyatāṃ vijayāya vaḥ |
0062-2 yasyaikapalitabhrāntiṃ karotpadyāpi jāhnavī | |
0063-1 sa pātu vo yasya jaṭākalāpe
0063-2 sthitaḥ śaśāṅkaḥ sphuṭahāragauraḥ |
0063-3 nīlotpalānāmiva nālapuñje
0063-4 nidrāyamāṇaḥ śaradīva haṃsaḥ | |
0064-1 diśyātsa śītakiraṇābharaṇaḥ śivaṃ vo
0064-2 yasyottamāṅgabhuvi visphuradūrmipakṣā |
0064-3 haṃsīva nirmalaśaśāṅkakalāmṛṇāla-
0064-4 kandārthinī surasarinnabhasaḥ papāta | |
0065-1 śreyāṃsi vo diśatu yasya sitābhraśubhrā
0065-2 vibhrājate surasaridvaramaulimālā |
0065-3 ūrdhvekṣaṇajvalanatāpavilīyamāna-
0065-4 candrāmṛtapravitatāmṛtavāhinīva | |
0066-1 cyutāmindorlekhāṃ ratikalahabhagnaṃ ca valayaṃ
0066-2 śanairekīkṛtya prahasitamukhī śailatanayā |
0066-3 avocadyaṃ paśyotyavatu sa śivaḥ sā ca girijā
0066-4 sa ca krīḍācandro daśanakiraṇāpūritatanuḥ | |
0067-1 eṣā te hara kā sugātri katamā mūrdhni sthitā kiṃ jaṭā
0067-2 haṃsaḥ kiṃ bhajate jaṭāṃ nahi śaśī candro jalaṃ sevate |
0067-3 mugdho bhūtiriyaṃ kutotra salilaṃ bhūtistaraṅgāyate
0067-4 evaṃ yo vinigūhate tripathagāṃ pāyātsa vaḥ śaṃkaraḥ | |
0068-1 āśleṣādharavimbacumbanasukhālāpasmitānyāsatāṃ
0068-2 dūre tāvadidaṃ mitho na sulabhaṃ jātaṃ mukhālokanaṃ |
0068-3 itthaṃ vyarthakṛtaikadehaghaṭanopanyāsayorāvayoḥ
0068-4 keyaṃ premaviḍambanetyavatu vaḥ smerordhanārīśvaraḥ | |
0069-1 mātarjīva kimetadañjalipuṭe tātena gopāyyate
0069-2 vatsa svādu phalaṃ prayacchati na me gatvā gṛhāṇa svayaṃ |
0069-3 mātraivaṃ prahite gṛhe vighaṭayatyākṛṣya saṃdhyāñjaliṃ
0069-4 śaṃbhorbhinnasamādhiruddharabhaso hāsodgamaḥ pātu vaḥ | |
0070-1 ekaṃ cantacchadasya sphurati japavaśādardhamanyatprakopād-
0070-2 ekaḥ pāṇiḥ praṇantuṃ śirasi kṛtapadaḥ kṣeptumanyastameva |
0070-3 ekaṃ dhyānānnimīlatyaparamaviṣahaṃ vīkṣituṃ cakṣuritthaṃ
0070-4 tulyānicchāpi vāmā tanuravatu sa vo yasya saṃdhyāvasāne | |
0071-1 śailarājatanayāstanayagmavyāpṛtāsyayugalasya gṛhasya |
0071-2 śeṣavakrakamalāni malaṃ vo dugdhapānavidhurāṇi harantu | |
0072-1 karajālamapūrvaceṣṭitaṃ vastadabhīṣṭapradamastu tigmabhāsāḥ |
0072-2 kriyate bhavabandhanādvimuktiḥ praṇatānāmupasevitena yena | |
0073-1 yuṣmākamambaramaṇe prathame mayūkhās-
0073-2 te maṅgalaṃ vidadhatūdayarāgabhājaḥ |
0073-3 kurvanti ye divasajanmamahotsaveṣu
0073-4 sindūrapāṭalamukhīriva dikpuraṃdhrīḥ | |
0074-1 ābāhūdgatamaṇḍalāgrarucayaḥ saṃnaddhavakṣaḥsthalāḥ
0074-2 soṣmāṇo vraṇino vipakṣahṛdaypronmāthinaḥ karkaśāḥ |
0074-3 utsṛṣṭāmbaradṛṣṭavigrahabharā yasya smarāgresarā
0074-4 yodhā vāravadhūstanāśca na dadhuḥ kṣobhaṃ sa vovyājjinaḥ | |
0075-1 kiṃ syādbhāsvānna bhānoramṛtaghanarasasyandinaḥ santi pādāḥ
0075-2 kiṃ vā rākāśaśāṅko nahi tuhinaruciḥ kutracinniṣkalaṅkaḥ |
0075-3 sākṣāccintāmaṇiḥ kiṃ vipulaphalamaṇeḥ saukumāryaṃ kutastyaṃ
0075-4 saṃdehānmugdhadhībhiḥ prathamamiti muneḥ pātu dṛṣṭaṃ vapurvaḥ | |
0076-1 ciramāviṣkṛtaprītibhītayaḥ pāntu vo dviṣāṃ |

1013-1 sāṃmukhyaṃ vastujātaṃ nayati nanu cidīśasya yaddarśanāḍhyaṃ
1013-2 netradvandvaṃ kilaitadvimalamiti tatonyāṅgasaṅgaṃ vihāya |
1013-3 ghrāṇaṃ vaṃśābhirāmaṃ parimalanirataṃ cakṣuṣormadhyabhāge
1013-4 nityaṃ līnaṃ na cāsminmṛgasi nayanayoḥ śvāsamāmuñca khinne | |
1014-1 etattasya mukhātkiyatkamalinīpattre kaṇaṃ pāthaso
1014-2 yanmuktāphalamityamaṃsta sa jaḍaḥ śṛṇvanyadasmādapi |
1014-3 aṅgulyagralaghukriyāpravilayinyādīyamāne śanais-
1014-4 tatroḍḍīya gate hahetyanudinaṃ nidrāti nāntaḥśucā | |
1015-1 āstetraiva sarasyaho bata kiyānsaṃtoṣapakṣagraho
1015-2 haṃsasyāsya manāṅna dhāvati matiḥ śrīdhāmni padme kvacit |
1015-3 suptodyāpi vibudhyate na taditastāvatpratīkṣāmahe
1015-4 velāmityuṣasi priyā madhulihaḥ soḍhuṃ tu eva kṣamāḥ | |
1016-1 vātāhāratayā jagadviṣadharairāśvāsya niḥśeṣitaṃ
1016-2 te grastāḥ punarabhratoyakaṇikātīvravratairbarhibhiḥ |
1016-3 tepi krūracamūrucarmavasanairnītāḥ kṣayaṃ lubdhakair-
1016-4 dambhasya sphuritaṃ vidannapi jano jālmo guṇānīhate | |
1017-1 nāmāpyanyatarornimīlitamabhūttattāvadunmīlitaṃ
1017-2 prasthāne skhalataḥ svavartmani vidheranyairgṛhītaḥ karaḥ |
1017-3 lokaścāyamadṛṣṭadarśanadaśādṛgvaiśasāduddhṛto
1017-4 yuktaṃ kāṣṭhika lūnavānyadasitāmāmrālimākālikīṃ | |
1018-1 ūḍhā yena mahādhuraḥ suviṣame mārge sadaikākinā
1018-2 soḍho yena kadācideva na nije goṣṭhenyaśauṇḍadhvaniḥ |
1018-3 āsīdyaśca gavāṃ gaṇasya tilakastasyaiva saṃpratyaho
1018-4 dhikkaṣṭaṃ dhavalasya jātajaraso goḥ paṇyamuddhoṣyate | |
1019-1 bhekena kvaṇatā saroṣaparuṣaṃ yatkṛṣṇasarpānane
1019-2 dātuṃ karṇacapeṭamujjhitabhiyā hastaḥ samullāsitaḥ |
1019-3 yaccādh_oṃukhamakṣiṇī pidadhatā nāgena tatra sthitaṃ
1019-4 tatsarvaṃ viṣamantriṇo bhagavataḥ kasyāpi līlāyitaṃ | |
1020-1 nityaṃ tīrthe nivāsaḥ prakṛtiratitarāṃ snigdhamugdhasvabhāvā
1020-2 vṛttirdaivāddhi vaktre gagananipatitairnirmalairvārileśaiḥ |
1020-3 itthaṃ sarvaṃ vilokya prakaṭamiha time mugdhalokena loke
1020-4 sādhutvaṃ darśitaṃ te bahirabahiramī kaṇṭakāḥ kena dṛṣṭāḥ | |
1021-1 mṛtyorāsyamivātataṃ dhanuramī cāśīviṣābhāḥ śarāḥ
1021-2 śikṣā sāpi jitārjunā pratibhayaṃ sarvāṅganimnā gatiḥ |
1021-3 antaḥ krauryamaho śaṭhasya madhuraṃ hā hāri geyaṃ mukhe
1021-4 vyādhasyāsya yathā bhaviṣyati tathā manye vanaṃ nirmṛgaṃ | |
1022-1 dhigvy_oṃno mahimānametu dalaśaḥ proccaistadīyaṃ padaṃ
1022-2 nindyāṃ daivagatiṃ prayātvabhavanistasyāstu śūnyasya vā |
1022-3 yenotkṣiptakarasya naṣṭamahasaḥ śrāntasya saṃtāpino
1022-4 mitrasyāpi nirāśrayasya na kṛtaṃ dhṛtyai karālambanaṃ | |
1023-1 digdāhaikarate vanāntakara te jvālā na me rocate
1023-2 dugdhaṃ svāśrayamudyatasya bhavato necchanti vṛddhiṃ janāḥ |
1023-3 mūlānyasya mahībhṛto dalayituṃ durvedhasā nirmitaḥ
1023-4 ko vā na tvayi śaṅkate khala jagatkhedāvahe dāva he | |
1024-1 kṣutkṣāmeṇa kathaṃ kathaṃcidaniśaṃ gātraṃ kṛśaṃ bibhratā
1024-2 bhrāntaṃ yena gṛhe gṛhe gṛhavatāmucchiṣṭapiṇḍārthinā |
1024-3 asthnaḥ khaṇḍamavāpya daivapatitaṃ śūnyāṃ trilokīmimāṃ
1024-4 manvāno dhigaho sa eva saramāputrodya siṃhāyate | |
1025-1 śuṣkasnāyuvasāvasekamalinaṃ nirmāṃsamapyasthi goḥ
1025-2 śvā labdhā paritoṣameti na tu tattasya kṣudhaḥ śāntaye |
1025-3 siṃho jambukamaṅkamāgatamapi tyaktvā nihanti dvipaṃ
1025-4 sarvaḥ kṛchragatopi vāñchati janaḥ sattvānurūpaṃ phalaṃ | |
1026-1 kāluṣyaṃ payasāṃ vilokya śanakairuḍḍīya haṃsā gatā
1026-2 dhārājarjarakesarāsphuṭarucaḥ padmā nimignā jale |
1026-3 sā sarvartusukhāvatārapadavī channā tṛṇairnūtanaiḥ
1026-4 kaṣṭaṃ tādṛgapi svabhāvavimalaṃ vṛdchyaiva naṣṭaṃ saraḥ | |
1027-1 ye saṃtoṣasukhaprabuddhamanasasteṣāmabhinno mṛdo
1027-2 yepyete dhanalobhasaṃkuladhiyasteṣāṃ tu dūre nṛṇāṃ |
1027-3 itthaṃ kasya kṛte kṛtaḥ sa vidhinā tādṛkpadaṃ saṃpadāṃ
1027-4 svātmanyeva samāptahemamahimā merurna me rocate | |
1028-1 dravyāṇāmadharottaravyatikaro bhagnāśayānāmadho
1028-2 bījānāṃ nayanaṃ svayaṃ ca nijavacchidrakriyānveṣaṇaṃ |
1028-3 vyūhābandhavidhāyibhirgatabhayairmugdhaprasuptārbhakaṃ
1028-4 śūnyaṃ prāpya nivāsamākhubhiraho kiṃ kiṃ na yadyatkṛtaṃ | |
1029-1 anyonyasya layaṃ bhayādiva mahābhūteṣu yāteṣvalaṃ
1029-2 kalpānte parameka eva sa taruḥ skandhoccayairjṛmbhate |
1029-3 vinyasya trijaganti kukṣikuhare devena yasyāsyate
1029-4 śākhāgre śiśuneva sevitajalakrīḍāvilāsālasaṃ | |trivikramasya
1030-1 trailokyopakṛtiprasaktamanaso devasya śaṃbhoḥ priyā
1030-2 jātā śailakule varairabhimatairānandayantī surān |

1030-4 vindhyasyonnatimātanoti na nijāṃ daivasya kīdṛgbalaṃ | |bhā. amṛtadattasya
1031-1 kiṃ tvaṃ hālika mūḍhadhīrhataphalaṃ mā mā kṛthā lāṅgalaṃ
1031-2 kṣetraṃ naiva bhavatyadhaḥ kaṭhinatā naivātra dṛṣṭā tvayā |
1031-3 ullekhopi na jāyatetra virama kleśaḥ phalaṃ kevalaṃ
1031-4 nirbījā bahavo gatāśca satataṃ dṛṣṭāḥ śrutā vā na kiṃ | |kasyāpi
1032-1 koyaṃ bhrāntiprakārastava pavana ghanāvaskarasthānajātaṃ

1032-4 kenopāyena sahyo vapuṣi malinatādoṣa eṣa tvayaiva | |bhā. amṛtadattasya
1033-1 jātaḥ kūrmaḥ sa ekaḥ pṛthubhuvanabharāyārpitaṃ yena pṛṣṭhaṃ

1038-1 ayaṃ sa bhuvanatrayaprathitasaṃyamaḥ śaṃkaro

1038-4 kareṇa paripīḍayañjayati jātahāsaḥ smaraḥ | |
1039-1 bhrūśārṅgākṛṣṭamuktāḥ kuvalayamadhupavy_oṃalakṣmīmuṣo ye
